<p>The <b>Netherlands national cricket team</b> is the team that represents the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Kingdom of the Netherlands</a> and is administered by the <a href="/wiki/Koninklijke_Nederlandse_Cricket_Bond" title="Koninklijke Nederlandse Cricket Bond">Koninklijke Nederlandse Cricket Bond</a> (<i>Royal Dutch Cricket Association</i>).
</p><p>Cricket has been played in the Netherlands since at least the 19th century, and in the 1860s was considered a major sport in the country. Other sports – notably <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> – have long since surpassed cricket in popularity amongst the Dutch, but today there are around 6,000 cricketers in the Netherlands. The first national association, the forerunner of today's Royal Dutch Cricket Association, was formed in 1883 and the Netherlands achieved Associate Membership of the <a href="/wiki/International_Cricket_Council" title="International Cricket Council">International Cricket Council</a> (ICC) in 1966.
</p><p>The Netherlands have taken part in all eleven <a href="/wiki/ICC_World_Cup_Qualifier" title="ICC World Cup Qualifier">ICC Trophy/World Cup Qualifier</a> tournaments, winning the competition in Canada in 2001 and finishing as runners-up twice (in 1986 and 1990). The Netherlands also participated in the 1996, 2003, 2007 and 2011 <a href="/wiki/Cricket_World_Cup" title="Cricket World Cup">Cricket World Cups</a>, and from 1996 onwards the national team entered the English domestic <a href="/wiki/NatWest_Trophy" class="mw-redirect" title="NatWest Trophy">NatWest Trophy</a> competition (and its successor, the <a href="/wiki/C%26G_Trophy" class="mw-redirect" title="C&amp;G Trophy">C&amp;G Trophy</a>). In 2004 they played <a href="/wiki/First-class_cricket" title="First-class cricket">first-class cricket</a> in the <a href="/wiki/ICC_Intercontinental_Cup" title="ICC Intercontinental Cup">ICC Intercontinental Cup</a>, drawing with <a href="/wiki/Scottish_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Scottish cricket team">Scotland</a> in Aberdeen and then going down to an <a href="/wiki/The_result_in_cricket" class="mw-redirect" title="The result in cricket">innings defeat</a> against <a href="/wiki/Irish_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Irish cricket team">Ireland</a> in <a href="/wiki/Deventer" title="Deventer">Deventer</a>.
</p><p>The Netherlands enjoyed full <a href="/wiki/One_Day_International" title="One Day International">One Day International</a> status from 1 January 2006 until 1 February 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> They regained <a href="/wiki/Twenty20_International" title="Twenty20 International">Twenty20 International</a> status in June 2014, having played their first match in this format in 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-espncricinfoci_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espncricinfoci-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> The Netherlands regained their ODI status after the conclusion of the <a href="/wiki/2018_Cricket_World_Cup_Qualifier" title="2018 Cricket World Cup Qualifier">2018 Cricket World Cup Qualifier</a> in March 2018. They had guaranteed this status before the tournament as a result of winning the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9317_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Championship" title="2015–17 ICC World Cricket League Championship">2015–17 ICC World Cricket League Championship</a> and thus qualifying for the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9322_ICC_ODI_League" class="mw-redirect" title="2020–22 ICC ODI League">2020–22 ICC ODI League</a>, and will retain the status until the <a href="/wiki/2022_Cricket_World_Cup_Qualifier" title="2022 Cricket World Cup Qualifier">2022 Cricket World Cup Qualifier</a>.
</p><p>In April 2018, the ICC decided to grant full <a href="/wiki/Twenty20_International" title="Twenty20 International">Twenty20 International</a> (T20I) status to all its members. Therefore, all <a href="/wiki/Twenty20" title="Twenty20">Twenty20</a> matches played between the Netherlands and other <a href="/wiki/List_of_International_Cricket_Council_members" title="List of International Cricket Council members">ICC members</a> after 1 January 2019 will be a full T20I.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Pieter_Seelaar" title="Pieter Seelaar">Pieter Seelaar</a> is the current team captain.<sup id="cite_ref-Apr18_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Apr18-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="19th_century">19th century</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 19th century">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Cricket was introduced to the Netherlands by British soldiers during the <a href="/wiki/Napoleonic_Wars" title="Napoleonic Wars">Napoleonic Wars</a> in the 19th century.<sup id="cite_ref-ref1_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ref1-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Further clubs came into existence in the 1870s. The Netherlands national team played their first game in 1881. They fielded 22 players against an <a href="/wiki/Uxbridge" title="Uxbridge">Uxbridge</a> Cricket Club XI, but still lost by an innings. The Dutch Cricket Union was formed in 1883, with 18 member clubs, four of which are still in existence today.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The first national tournament was held the following year, and was won by <a href="/wiki/Haagsche_CC" class="mw-redirect" title="Haagsche CC">Haagsche CC</a>. English touring teams then began visiting in 1886 including one in 1891 that featured the author of <a href="/wiki/Sherlock_Holmes" title="Sherlock Holmes">Sherlock Holmes</a>, Sir <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Conan_Doyle" title="Arthur Conan Doyle">Arthur Conan Doyle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 1894, the Gentlemen of Holland were the first Dutch team to visit England. The tour included a game against the <a href="/wiki/Marylebone_Cricket_Club" title="Marylebone Cricket Club">MCC</a> at <a href="/wiki/Lord%27s" title="Lord&#39;s">Lord's</a>, which the MCC won by an innings and 169 runs.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Tours by English sides continued for the rest of the 1890s, which also saw the emergence of <a href="/wiki/Carst_Posthuma" title="Carst Posthuma">Carst Posthuma</a>, who was later the first Dutch player to play first class cricket.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He took 2339 wickets at an average of 8.66 in his career in the Netherlands.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1900s_to_1910s">1900s to 1910s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 1900s to 1910s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>1901 saw another visit to England by the Gentlemen of Holland. They played five games on the tour, drawing two and losing the remainder.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> 1905 saw the first international game against <a href="/wiki/Belgian_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Belgian cricket team">Belgium</a>, which finished in a draw.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Cricket began a decline in popularity in the first decade of the 20th century, particularly amongst young athletes, due, in part, to the Dutch sympathizing with the Boers in the Boer War and therefore not being attracted to a game with links to England.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 1910, the Dutch team visited <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a> to take part in an exhibition tournament, which also featured the MCC, Belgium and <a href="/wiki/French_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="French cricket team">France</a>. They lost to the MCC by 2 wickets,<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> and to France by 63 runs,<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> but beat Belgium by 116 runs.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a>, in which the Netherlands remained neutral, large numbers of British officers were <a href="/wiki/Internment" title="Internment">interned</a> in the country, and many of these joined local cricket clubs. A team made up of these players even won the Dutch championship in 1918.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1920s_to_1940s">1920s to 1940s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 1920s to 1940s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Flamingos, a Dutch touring side, was formed in 1921, and later made several tours of England. Tours by English teams also continued in this period. The 1930s are said to be the heyday of Dutch cricket. In 1934, the first Dutch women's league was formed, and the women's national team played two games against Australia in 1937, losing heavily in both. Cricket was of course curtailed after the German invasion in 1940.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1950s_to_1980s">1950s to 1980s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 1950s to 1980s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The 1950s saw visits to the Netherlands by <a href="/wiki/Australia_national_cricket_team" title="Australia national cricket team">Australia</a> and the <a href="/wiki/West_Indies_cricket_team" title="West Indies cricket team">West Indies</a>, in addition to their first match against <a href="/wiki/Denmark_national_cricket_team" title="Denmark national cricket team">Denmark</a>. In 1958, the Cricket Board received a Royal Charter, and became the "Koninklijke Nederlandse Cricket Bond", a name which it retains to this day.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In August 1964, the Netherlands achieved their first victory against a Test-playing nation when they beat Australia by three wickets at The Hague.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> They were rewarded with <a href="/wiki/List_of_International_Cricket_Council_members#Associate_Members" title="List of International Cricket Council members">associate membership of the ICC</a> two years later.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="width: 100%; clear:both">

</div>
<p>The first two <a href="/wiki/ICC_Trophy" class="mw-redirect" title="ICC Trophy">ICC Trophy</a> tournaments, in 1979 and 1982, brought little success to the Dutch, who were eliminated in the first round in both tournaments. But in the <a href="/wiki/1986_ICC_Trophy" title="1986 ICC Trophy">1986 tournament</a>, they finished as runners-up to <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe_national_cricket_team" title="Zimbabwe national cricket team">Zimbabwe</a>. The same year, <a href="/wiki/Paul-Jan_Bakker" title="Paul-Jan Bakker">Paul-Jan Bakker</a> became the first Dutch player to play county cricket.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> In 1989, the Dutch beat a strong <a href="/wiki/England_cricket_team" title="England cricket team">England XI</a> that included two future England captains, <a href="/wiki/Alec_Stewart" title="Alec Stewart">Alec Stewart</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nasser_Hussain" title="Nasser Hussain">Nasser Hussain</a>, by 3 runs.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1990s">1990s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 1990s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In 1990 the Netherlands hosted the <a href="/wiki/1990_ICC_Trophy" title="1990 ICC Trophy">ICC Trophy</a>, the first such tournament outside England, and again finished runners-up to Zimbabwe.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> In 1991 they achieved a five-wicket win over a West Indies XI,<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> followed in 1993 by a seven-wicket win over an England XI<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> and in 1994 a nine-wicket win over a <a href="/wiki/South_Africa_national_cricket_team" title="South Africa national cricket team">South Africa XI</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> In 1994 the Dutch finally qualified for the <a href="/wiki/Cricket_World_Cup" title="Cricket World Cup">World Cup</a>, after finishing third in <a href="/wiki/1994_ICC_Trophy" title="1994 ICC Trophy">that year's ICC Trophy</a>. In the <a href="/wiki/1996_Cricket_World_Cup" title="1996 Cricket World Cup">World Cup</a> itself in 1996, they were eliminated in the first round, but performed with some credit in their game against England.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="width: 100%; clear:both">
<table style="float:left; width:15%; table-layout:fixed; border-style:none">

<table style="float:right; width:32%; overflow:hidden; border-style:none">

<div style="clear:both; font-style: italic;">  </div>
</div>
<p>1995 saw the Netherlands enter the <a href="/wiki/Friends_Provident_Trophy" title="Friends Provident Trophy">NatWest Trophy</a> for the first time. They took part in this tournament for ten years, and their best performance came in <a href="/wiki/1999_NatWest_Trophy" title="1999 NatWest Trophy">1999</a> when they reached the fourth round, beating <a href="/wiki/Durham_County_Cricket_Club" title="Durham County Cricket Club">Durham</a> along the way.
</p><p>The Netherlands failed to qualify for the <a href="/wiki/1999_Cricket_World_Cup" title="1999 Cricket World Cup">1999 World Cup</a>, as they could only manage sixth in the <a href="/wiki/1997_ICC_Trophy" title="1997 ICC Trophy">1997 ICC Trophy</a>. However, the country hosted one World Cup match, between <a href="/wiki/Kenya_national_cricket_team" title="Kenya national cricket team">Kenya</a> and South Africa at <a href="/wiki/VRA_Cricket_Ground" title="VRA Cricket Ground">Amstelveen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Netherlands competed in the first <a href="/wiki/European_Cricket_Championship" title="European Cricket Championship">European Championship</a> in 1996, coming second. They have competed in every tournament since, winning in 1998 and 2000.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="21st_century">21st century</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 21st century">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2000.E2.80.932009"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2000–2009">2000–2009</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2000–2009">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>2001 finally saw the Netherlands win the ICC Trophy, beating <a href="/wiki/Namibian_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Namibian cricket team">Namibia</a> in the final in <a href="/wiki/Toronto" title="Toronto">Toronto</a>. They thus qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2003_Cricket_World_Cup" title="2003 Cricket World Cup">2003 World Cup</a>. They again failed to progress beyond the first round in the tournament, but recorded their first one-day international win over Namibia during the tournament. <a href="/wiki/Feiko_Kloppenburg" title="Feiko Kloppenburg">Feiko Kloppenburg</a> (with 121) and <a href="/wiki/Klaas-Jan_van_Noortwijk" title="Klaas-Jan van Noortwijk">Klaas-Jan van Noortwijk</a> (134 not out) scored the first two One Day International centuries in the side's history.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2005_ICC_Trophy" title="2005 ICC Trophy">2005 ICC Trophy</a>, the Netherlands finished 5th, qualifying for the <a href="/wiki/2007_Cricket_World_Cup" title="2007 Cricket World Cup">2007 Cricket World Cup</a>, and gaining one-day International status until the <a href="/wiki/2009_ICC_World_Cup_Qualifier" class="mw-redirect" title="2009 ICC World Cup Qualifier">2009 ICC World Cup Qualifier</a>. Their first one-day international with this new status was scheduled to be against <a href="/wiki/Kenyan_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Kenyan cricket team">Kenya</a> in March 2006; however this match was cancelled due to a Kenyan tour of <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>. Instead their first ODI with this status (and their twelfth overall) came against <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lankan_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Sri Lankan cricket team">Sri Lanka</a>; this was their first ODI at home. However Sri Lanka won the two match series 2–0, with a then-record ODI score of 443–9.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Dutch played their first Intercontinental Cup match of 2006 against <a href="/wiki/Kenyan_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Kenyan cricket team">Kenya</a> in Nairobi in March. The game was drawn, but the Netherlands gained six points for a first innings lead.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> In August, the Netherlands competed in Division One of the <a href="/wiki/European_Cricket_Championship" title="European Cricket Championship">European Championship</a>. They beat <a href="/wiki/Danish_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Danish cricket team">Denmark</a> and <a href="/wiki/Italian_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Italian cricket team">Italy</a>, but lost to <a href="/wiki/Scottish_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Scottish cricket team">Scotland</a> and their game against <a href="/wiki/Irish_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Irish cricket team">Ireland</a> was rained off. They finished third in the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-TL_11-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TL-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In November, the Dutch travelled to South Africa. They first played an Intercontinental Cup match against <a href="/wiki/Bermuda_national_cricket_team" title="Bermuda national cricket team">Bermuda</a>:   <a href="/wiki/David_Hemp" title="David Hemp">David Hemp</a> achieved what was then a competition record score of 247 <a href="/wiki/Not_out" title="Not out">not out</a> in the drawn match.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> This was followed by a triangular series against Bermuda and <a href="/wiki/Canada_national_cricket_team" title="Canada national cricket team">Canada</a>, which they won.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Their final game of 2006, also in South Africa, was an Intercontinental Cup game against Canada. They won the match by 7 wickets, with <a href="/wiki/Ryan_ten_Doeschate" title="Ryan ten Doeschate">Ryan ten Doeschate</a> setting a new competition record individual score of 259 not out.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In early 2007, they travelled to <a href="/wiki/Nairobi" title="Nairobi">Nairobi</a>, Kenya to take part in <a href="/wiki/2007_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_One" title="2007 ICC World Cricket League Division One">Division One</a> of the <a href="/wiki/World_Cricket_League" title="World Cricket League">World Cricket League</a>, finishing third out of six.<sup id="cite_ref-2007WCL1_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2007WCL1-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> This was followed by the <a href="/wiki/2007_Cricket_World_Cup" title="2007 Cricket World Cup">2007 World Cup</a> in the West Indies, where they were eliminated in the first round, though they did beat <a href="/wiki/Scotland_national_cricket_team" title="Scotland national cricket team">Scotland</a> along the way.<sup id="cite_ref-2007WC_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2007WC-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the World Cup, they underwent a period of transformation. Captain <a href="/wiki/Luuk_van_Troost" title="Luuk van Troost">Luuk van Troost</a> retired, as did <a href="/wiki/Tim_de_Leede" title="Tim de Leede">Tim de Leede</a> and their coach Peter Cantrell. <a href="/wiki/Daan_van_Bunge" title="Daan van Bunge">Daan van Bunge</a> also opted to take a break from international cricket, and the new coach opted not to retain the services of bowling coach <a href="/wiki/Ian_Pont" title="Ian Pont">Ian Pont</a>.
</p><p>In June 2007, they visited Canada, first winning an Intercontinental Cup match against Canada in <a href="/wiki/King_City,_Ontario" title="King City, Ontario">King City, Ontario</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> They then won the first ODI by 117 runs,<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> with the second one being abandoned.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> They then played a quadrangular series in Ireland, losing by ten wickets to the <a href="/wiki/West_Indies_cricket_team" title="West Indies cricket team">West Indies</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> and by one run to <a href="/wiki/Ireland_cricket_team" title="Ireland cricket team">Ireland</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> with the game against Scotland being abandoned due to rain.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In August 2008, The Netherlands participated in the <a href="/wiki/2009_ICC_World_Twenty20_Qualifier" class="mw-redirect" title="2009 ICC World Twenty20 Qualifier">2009 ICC World Twenty20 Qualifier</a>. This was their debut playing <a href="/wiki/Twenty20_International" title="Twenty20 International">Twenty20 International</a> matches.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> They finished in first place in Group B, based on their run-rate.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> After beating Scotland in the Semi-Finals,<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> the final was abandoned due to rain and the trophy was shared between The Netherlands and Ireland.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Netherlands caused a sensation in the cricketing world by beating England<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> in the opening match of the <a href="/wiki/ICC_World_Twenty20_2009" class="mw-redirect" title="ICC World Twenty20 2009">ICC World Twenty20 2009</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> whilst being 500/1 outsiders.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

</div>
<p>They lost their second match to the eventual winners Pakistan<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> and did not qualify for the super 8 stage based on run rate.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Netherlands_cricket_team.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Netherlands_cricket_team.jpg/220px-Netherlands_cricket_team.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="140" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Netherlands_cricket_team.jpg/330px-Netherlands_cricket_team.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Netherlands_cricket_team.jpg/440px-Netherlands_cricket_team.jpg 2x" data-file-width="668" data-file-height="425" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Netherlands_cricket_team.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Netherlands national cricket team at <a href="/wiki/Rotterdam" title="Rotterdam">Rotterdam</a>, <a href="/wiki/2010_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_One" title="2010 ICC World Cricket League Division One">ICC WCL Division One in 2010</a></div></div></div>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.93present"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2010–present">2010–present</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2010–present">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 20 July 2010, The Netherlands beat a full-member nation for the first time in an ODI. In a one-off match shortened by rain to 30 overs a side, they beat Bangladesh by 6 wickets.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> The win in combination with their winning percentage against other associate and affiliate nations resulted in The Netherlands being included in ICC's official ODI-rankings.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="width: 100%; clear:both">
<table style="float:left; width:15%; table-layout:fixed; border-style:none">
<tbody><tr>

<div style="clear:both; font-style: italic;">
<ul><li>Netherlands won the toss and elected to field.</li>
<li>Match reduced to 30 overs a side.<br />First ever ODI win for Netherlands over a full ICC Member team.</li></ul></div>
</div>
<p>On 22 February 2011, The Netherlands posted their highest ever total against a full-member nation, scoring 292 against England, batting first at the <a href="/wiki/2011_Cricket_World_Cup" title="2011 Cricket World Cup">2011 Cricket World Cup</a>. <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Ten_Doeschate" class="mw-redirect" title="Ryan Ten Doeschate">Ryan Ten Doeschate</a> top scored 119 from 110 balls. However, the Netherlands were unable to defend their strong total and failed to pull off a huge shock, England winning by 6 wickets with 2 overs to spare. They eventually failed to win any of their group matches and were last in their Group.
</p><p>In September 2011, Netherlands whitewashed <a href="/wiki/Kenya_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Kenya cricket team">Kenya</a> in a short two-match ODI series held at home.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2014_ICC_World_Twenty20" title="2014 ICC World Twenty20">2014 ICC World Twenty20</a>, Netherlands had one win and one loss before their final game. In order to go through on net run rate against <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Zimbabwe cricket team">Zimbabwe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ireland_national_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Ireland national cricket team">Ireland</a>, they needed to chase down Ireland's score in 14.2 overs or less. As Ireland scored 189, this seemed unlikely. However, strong and aggressive batting enabled them to score 193/4 in 13.5 overs, securing passage to the <a href="/wiki/2014_ICC_World_Twenty20_Super_10s" title="2014 ICC World Twenty20 Super 10s">2014 ICC World Twenty20 Super 10s</a>. Although they lost their first three games in the group, including a 39/10 against <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka_national_cricket_team" title="Sri Lanka national cricket team">Sri Lanka</a>, they pulled off an upset against <a href="/wiki/England_national_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="England national cricket team">England</a> in their last game.
</p>
<div style="width: 100%; background-color: transparent">

<p>In June 2014, Nepal along with <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Netherlands cricket team">Netherlands</a> granted <a href="/wiki/Twenty20_International" title="Twenty20 International">T20</a> status by the <a href="/wiki/International_Cricket_Council" title="International Cricket Council">ICC</a> board at the annual conference in <a href="/wiki/Melbourne" title="Melbourne">Melbourne</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-espncricinfoci_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espncricinfoci-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Twenty20_Internationals">Twenty20 Internationals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Twenty20 Internationals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Highest team total: 194/7 v. <a href="/wiki/Scotland_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Scotland cricket team">Scotland</a> on 16 September 2019 at <a href="/wiki/Malahide_Cricket_Club_Ground" title="Malahide Cricket Club Ground">Malahide Cricket Club Ground</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malahide" title="Malahide">Malahide</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Highest individual score: 96<a href="/wiki/Not_out" title="Not out">*</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pieter_Seelaar" title="Pieter Seelaar">Pieter Seelaar</a> v. <a href="/wiki/Scotland_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Scotland cricket team">Scotland</a> on 16 September 2019 at <a href="/wiki/Malahide_Cricket_Club_Ground" title="Malahide Cricket Club Ground">Malahide Cricket Club Ground</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malahide" title="Malahide">Malahide</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Best individual bowling figures: 5/19, <a href="/wiki/Ahsan_Malik_(cricketer)" title="Ahsan Malik (cricketer)">Ahsan Malik</a> v. <a href="/wiki/South_Africa_national_cricket_team" title="South Africa national cricket team">South Africa</a>, 27 March 2014 at <a href="/wiki/Zohur_Ahmed_Chowdhury_Stadium" title="Zohur Ahmed Chowdhury Stadium">Zohur Ahmed Chowdhury Stadium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chittagong" title="Chittagong">Chittagong</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Records">Other Records</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Other Records">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="ICC_Trophy">ICC Trophy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: ICC Trophy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Highest team total: 425/4 v. <a href="/wiki/Israeli_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Israeli cricket team">Israel</a>, 18 June 1986 at <a href="/wiki/Solihull" title="Solihull">Solihull</a>, England<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Highest individual innings: 169 not out, <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Gomes" title="Rupert Gomes">Rupert Gomes</a> v. <a href="/wiki/Israeli_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Israeli cricket team">Israel</a>, 4 June 1990 at <a href="/wiki/Amstelveen" title="Amstelveen">Amstelveen</a>, Netherlands<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Best innings bowling: 7/9, <a href="/wiki/Asim_Khan_(cricketer)" title="Asim Khan (cricketer)">Asim Khan</a> v. <a href="/wiki/East_and_Central_African_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="East and Central African cricket team">East &amp; Central Africa</a>, 24 March 1997 at <a href="/wiki/Royal_Military_College,_Kuala_Lumpur" class="mw-redirect" title="Royal Military College, Kuala Lumpur">Royal Military College, Kuala Lumpur</a>, Malaysia<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_players">Notable players</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Netherlands_national_cricket_team&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Notable players">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Update plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Update" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><img alt="Ambox current red.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/42px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png" decoding="async" width="42" height="34" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/63px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/84px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="360" data-file-height="290" /></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section needs to be <b>updated</b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">February 2019</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ryan_ten_doeschate.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Ryan_ten_doeschate.jpg/220px-Ryan_ten_doeschate.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="282" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Ryan_ten_doeschate.jpg/330px-Ryan_ten_doeschate.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Ryan_ten_doeschate.jpg/440px-Ryan_ten_doeschate.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1232" data-file-height="1580" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ryan_ten_doeschate.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Ryan_ten_Doeschate" title="Ryan ten Doeschate">Ryan ten Doeschate</a> currently holds the record for the highest batting average in ODI cricket.</div></div></div>
<p>Several Dutch cricketers have also played at first-class level elsewhere, the most successful of these probably being <a href="/wiki/Roland_Lefebvre" title="Roland Lefebvre">Roland Lefebvre</a> who played for <a href="/wiki/Somerset_County_Cricket_Club" title="Somerset County Cricket Club">Somerset</a> and <a href="/wiki/Glamorgan_County_Cricket_Club" title="Glamorgan County Cricket Club">Glamorgan</a> in English <a href="/wiki/County_cricket" title="County cricket">county cricket</a> as well as for <a href="/wiki/Canterbury_cricket_team" title="Canterbury cricket team">Canterbury</a> in New Zealand.
</p><p>Dutch players to have played first class cricket outside of the Intercontinental Cup include:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ryan_ten_Doeschate" title="Ryan ten Doeschate">Ryan ten Doeschate</a> – Playing for <a href="/wiki/Essex_Eagles" class="mw-redirect" title="Essex Eagles">Essex</a>, <a href="/wiki/Canterbury_Wizards" class="mw-redirect" title="Canterbury Wizards">Canterbury Wizards</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kolkata_Knight_Riders" title="Kolkata Knight Riders">Kolkata Knight Riders</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Mashonaland_Eagles" title="Mashonaland Eagles">Mashonaland Eagles</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dirk_Nannes" title="Dirk Nannes">Dirk Nannes</a> – who has played for the <a href="/wiki/Victorian_Bushrangers" class="mw-redirect" title="Victorian Bushrangers">Victorian Bushrangers</a> in Australia, the <a href="/wiki/Delhi_Daredevils" class="mw-redirect" title="Delhi Daredevils">Delhi Daredevils</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Challengers_Bangalore" title="Royal Challengers Bangalore">Royal Challengers Bangalore</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Chennai_Super_Kings" title="Chennai Super Kings">Chennai Super Kings</a> in the IPL, and has played <a href="/wiki/List_of_Australia_Twenty20_International_cricketers" title="List of Australia Twenty20 International cricketers">T20I</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Australia_ODI_cricketers" title="List of Australia ODI cricketers">ODI</a> cricket for Australia.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nolan_Clarke" title="Nolan Clarke">Nolan Clarke</a> – who played for <a href="/wiki/Barbados" title="Barbados">Barbados</a> from 1969/70 until 1976/77.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tom_Cooper_(cricketer)" title="Tom Cooper (cricketer)">Tom Cooper</a> – who currently plays first class cricket for <a href="/wiki/South_Australia_cricket_team" title="South Australia cricket team">South Australia</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Michael_Swart" title="Michael Swart">Michael Swart</a> - who played for <a href="/wiki/Western_Australia_cricket_team" title="Western Australia cricket team"> Western Australia</a> from 2010 until 2011.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Paul-Jan_Bakker" title="Paul-Jan Bakker">Paul-Jan Bakker</a> – who played for <a href="/wiki/Hampshire_County_Cricket_Club" title="Hampshire County Cricket Club">Hampshire</a> from 1986 until 1992.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alexei_Kervezee" title="Alexei Kervezee">Alexei Kervezee</a> – Playing for <a href="/wiki/Worcestershire_County_Cricket_Club" title="Worcestershire County Cricket Club">Worcestershire</a> since 2007.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bill_Glerum" title="Bill Glerum">Bill Glerum</a> – who played one first class game for the Free Foresters in 1957.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carst_Posthuma" title="Carst Posthuma">Carst Posthuma</a> – who played five first class games for <a href="/wiki/London_County_Cricket_Club" title="London County Cricket Club">London County Cricket Club</a> in 1903.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Darron_Reekers" title="Darron Reekers">Darron Reekers</a> – who played three first-class games for <a href="/wiki/Otago" title="Otago">Otago</a> in 1997/98 and List A matches for both Otago and Canterbury (1994/95-2001/02).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Daan_van_Bunge" title="Daan van Bunge">Daan van Bunge</a> – who played for <a href="/wiki/Middlesex_County_Cricket_Club" title="Middlesex County Cricket Club">Middlesex</a> in 2004.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Andre_van_Troost" title="Andre van Troost">Andre van Troost</a> – who played for <a href="/wiki/Somerset_County_Cricket_Club" title="Somerset County Cricket Club">Somerset</a> from 1991 to 1998, and for <a href="/wiki/Griqualand_West" title="Griqualand West">Griqualand West</a> in the 1994/95 season in South Africa.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bastiaan_Zuiderent" title="Bastiaan Zuiderent">Bas Zuiderent</a> – who played for <a href="/wiki/Sussex_County_Cricket_Club" title="Sussex County Cricket Club">Sussex</a> from 2001 to 2003.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Timm_van_der_Gugten" title="Timm van der Gugten">Timm van der Gugten</a> – Played for <a href="/wiki/New_South_Wales_cricket_team" title="New South Wales cricket team">New South Wales</a> and others in Australia and New Zealand. Now playing for <a href="/wiki/Glamorgan_County_Cricket_Club" title="Glamorgan County Cricket Club">Glamorgan</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Logan_van_Beek" title="Logan van Beek">Logan van Beek</a> - who currently plays for <a href="/wiki/Wellington_Firebirds" class="mw-redirect" title="Wellington Firebirds">Wellington Firebirds</a> and previously represented <a href="/wiki/Canterbury_Wizards" class="mw-redirect" title="Canterbury Wizards">Canterbury Wizards</a></li></ul>
<p><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
